Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: Post-training quantization (PTQ) of diffusion transformers (DiTs) to W4A4 severely degrades output quality, because activations entering each linear layer contain outliers that 4-bit formats cannot represent. The standard fix applies an invertible linear transform to the activations and its inverse to the weights before quantizing both. Normalization layers between blocks force this transform to run online at every denoising step, making its inference computation cost the binding design constraint. Existing options trade quantization quality for inference cost: per-channel scaling (SmoothQuant) is computationally cheap but impacts the magnitude of the channels, which can harm quantization accuracy; fixed Hadamard transforms yield better quantization accuracy but require large block sizes that incur a high online cost; learned full-$d$ invertible transforms calibrate best but entail a prohibitive dense $d \times d$ matrix multiplication (GEMM) per layer per step.
  We propose KroQuant, a PTQ method that applies a learned Kronecker-structured invertible transform to each 32-element block of the activation, storing less than half the parameters of per-channel scaling. The block-local structure runs as small tensor-core GEMMs, and on an MI350 GPU the KroQuant quantizer kernel is up to $14\%$ faster than the SmoothQuant kernel. Offline LoRaQ weight calibration then absorbs the residual per-weight quantization error. On PixArt-$Σ$, SANA, and FLUX.1-schnell at W4A4 (MXFP4e2), KroQuant produces outputs closer to the FP reference than SVDQuant and LoRaQ on MJHQ-30K and SDCI, while preserving or improving image quality.

### [121] [Windowed-MTP: Removing the Full-Context Draft-KV Tax at Million-Token Context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21535)
*Alagappan Valliappan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Summary generation failed


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Conclusion: Conclusion extraction failed

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates autoregressive generation by having a cheap draft propose tokens that a target verifies in parallel. Frontier models increasingly ship a built-in Multi-Token-Prediction (MTP/NEXTN) draft head under the assumption that the draft is negligibly cheap. At million-token context this breaks: an MTP draft head typically runs full attention over the entire KV cache at every draft step, so its read grows linearly with context and comes to dominate the draft cost -- precisely where speculation is most valuable. The effect compounds with draft length (a deep native draft can turn net-negative, slower than no speculation) and sharpens under hybrid/linear-attention targets, where cheaper verification leaves the draft's full-attention read exposed. We apply a StreamingLLM-style sliding window plus attention sink to the draft's attention only (Windowed-MTP), leaving full-attention verification intact. It is training-free, drop-in, and lossless by construction: the full-attention target still decides every accepted token, so windowing changes only which tokens are proposed, never which are accepted. It bounds the draft's KV working set to a constant, dropping ~99% of KV entries at 1M. Across three architecture families (Qwen GDN-MoE 35B/122B and a Mamba2-hybrid NoPE 120B) at 1M context on a single GPU in SGLang, windowing cuts the per-decode-step cost over the shipping native MTP draft by +28% to +44%, an input-invariant margin that widens with context. Since per-token latency is this cost divided by acceptance length, at matched acceptance end-to-end decode latency improves by the same amount, and more where windowing also lifts acceptance, while preserving the target's verified output distribution. Finally, the unread draft KV -- 7.7-11% of total KV at 1M -- is reclaimed via a compact ring buffer at no acceptance or quality cost.

</details>

### [124] [Beyond Sufficiency: Time Series Explanation with Counterfactual Necessity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21573)

Abstract: Faithful explanations of time-series classifiers should identify subsequences that are not only sufficient to preserve a black-box model's prediction, but also necessary for maintaining it. However, existing sufficiency-oriented methods can assign high importance to spurious subsequences that support the prediction without being essential to the model's decision. We introduce \textbf{TimePNS}, a necessity-aware framework for time-series explanation. Inspired by Pearl's counterfactual notion of necessity, TimePNS assesses whether a temporal factor is necessary by intervening on it and measuring whether the original prediction is disrupted. The framework adopts a two-stage design. Stage I learns an identifiable causal generative process together with a sufficiency-oriented explanation mask. Stage II performs counterfactual interventions on temporal factors to derive necessity signals, which supervise a temporal gate that refines the initial explanation by suppressing non-essential components and emphasizing counterfactually necessary ones. Experiments on synthetic and real-world time-series benchmarks show that TimePNS more accurately identifies decision-critical subsequences and consistently improves sufficiency-necessity trade-offs over strong baselines.

### [125] [Expanding Flow Maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21585)
*Sophia Tang,Pranam Chatterjee*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Motivation analysis unavailable

Method: Method extraction failed

Result: Result analysis unavailable

Abstract: Flow-based generative models have enabled remarkable progress in fast and controllable generation across continuous and discrete state spaces, yet existing parameterizations are constrained to fixed dimensions or fixed sequence lengths. Here, we introduce Expanding Generative Flows (EFlows), which define flows between distributions of increasing dimensionality along an expanding interpolant that grows the state by augmenting it with conditional noise. Building on this construction, we propose Expanding Flow Maps (EFMs), a new class of flow maps that distill the expanding interpolant into efficient few-step generative models. Each EFM factors the map between any two timesteps into two learnable operations: an expand operator, which augments the state space with new coordinates or tokens conditioned on the current state, and a transport map, which pushes the expanded state forward along the interpolant. Composing these operators yields a single map that jointly expands and denoises the state, recovering existing fixed-canvas flows and flow maps as the special case in which the expand operator is the identity. We further extend the framework to the discrete simplex, enabling variable-size graph generation and variable-length sequence generation. Across both continuous and discrete modalities, we establish EFlows and EFMs as a principled framework for settings in which output size is itself a learned, controllable degree of freedom.

Abstract: We develop a hierarchical order-resolved relaxation model for a fixed D3Q125 discrete-velocity kinetic formulation. Conventional adaptive collision models often use one scalar rarefaction or nonequilibrium indicator for all retained moment orders, thereby coupling distinct kinetic sectors. Here, a shared macroscopic-gradient background is combined separately with second-, third-, and fourth-order thermodynamic nonequilibrium indicators to define effective measures K2, K3, and K4, each driving its own log-Gaussian relaxation spectrum.

Homogeneous mixed-order, amplitude, and composition tests show lower residual nonequilibrium than a common-sensor model while preserving positive populations. These results establish the mechanism and numerical behavior of order-resolved activation on a fixed velocity set; independent kinetic-reference validation is still required before claiming universal accuracy improvement.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的Jacobi方法主要适用于对称/Hermitian矩阵或正规矩阵，对于一般复矩阵的特征值问题缺乏高效高精度的求解方法。该研究旨在将Jacobi型方法推广到一般复矩阵，同时解决收敛区域有限和初始矩阵需接近对角形式的问题，使方法具有更广泛的适用性。

Method: 1) 采用初等三角相似变换逐次消去选定的非对角线元素；2) 给出渐近二次收敛性的新证明，并推导显式可验证的收敛区域界；3) 提出两种基于理论收敛结果的预条件器，以低精度计算预条件器，相似变换以工作精度或更高精度应用，主算法在工作精度下运行。

Result: 新的收敛性证明提供了可验证的收敛界；预条件策略使得方法不再局限于接近对角形式的矩阵；数值实验表明算法鲁棒且能产生非常精确的特征值。

Conclusion: 该Jacobi型方法结合低精度预条件策略，能够高效且高精度地求解一般复矩阵的特征值问题，具有良好的鲁棒性和实用性。

Abstract: The paper studies a Jacobi-type method for the eigenvalue problem of general complex matrices with simple eigenvalues. The method applies elementary triangular similarity transformations in order to annihilate selected off-diagonal elements and, when convergent, produces highly accurate eigenvalues. We give a new proof of its asymptotic quadratic convergence and derive an explicit, verifiable bound that describes the region in which this convergence is guaranteed. To make the method applicable well beyond matrices already close to the diagonal form, we introduce a preconditioning strategy. We use two types of preconditioners, both based on theoretical convergence results. The preconditioner is computed at lower precision to reduce computational cost, the associated similarity transformation is applied either at working or at higher precision, to preserve spectral information, while the main algorithm performs at working precision. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the resulting algorithm is robust and produces very accurate eigenvalues.

### [129] [An unfitted boundary algebraic equation method with Calderón preconditioning for 2D Stokes flow in irregular geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21295)
*Wenjun Ying,Qing Xia*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present an unfitted boundary algebraic equation method for the two-dimensional exterior/interior Stokes equations on a staggered MAC grid. By constructing an explicit free-space pair of velocity and pressure lattice Green's functions (LGFs) from free-space Laplace LGFs, we represent homogeneous fields using sources supported exclusively on thin staggered boundary layers. This formulation imposes physical Dirichlet data at cut points via local interpolation, while sampled-normal rank updates remove hydrostatic null modes associated with single or multiple obstacles. The workflow parallels that of classical boundary integral formulations and requires no artificial boundary conditions for exterior flows, but follows a discretize-then-represent route and does not require singular/near-singular quadrature. The resulting dense boundary system is solved via GMRES, utilizing a componentwise discrete Calderón preconditioner built from the scalar Laplace kernel and padded FFTs for fast volume convolutions. Extensive numerical validation, including multiply connected domains, narrow gaps, and Moffatt eddies, confirms discrete incompressibility to solver accuracy and recovers the expected Moffatt eddy scaling. We achieve second-order velocity and pressure convergence and bound maximum discrete divergence within numerical accuracy. The discrete Calderón preconditioner reduces the condition number by orders of magnitude and yields nearly mesh-independent conditioning in exterior configurations, while remaining effective---though more demanding---for narrow-gap and fine-grid interior problems.

Abstract: In this communication we propose a discrete Cosserat rod formulation in which a slender elastic rod is represented as a chain of rigid bodies (nodes) coupled by compliant elastic forces and moments acting between adjacent node pairs. Discrete dilatation, shear, torsion and curvature strain measures are evaluated from the relative kinematics of each node pair, while the constitutive behavior is expressed in compliance form through independent stress degrees of freedom. We show that the resulting model arises rigorously from a mixed Petrov--Galerkin Cosserat rod finite element formulation (FEM) at linear kinematic interpolation order when the internal virtual work is integrated by the midpoint rule and the external and inertial contributions by the trapezoidal rule. The proposed formulation inherits the robustness and the absence of locking from the underlying mixed FEM while simultaneously exposing a two-node coupling structure that mirrors discrete rod models from the computer graphics community. This is in sharp contrast to the dense coupling of strain-parameterized reduced-order models often used in soft robotic applications. Abstract: This paper considers a class of charged-particle dynamics problems in which the particle is subjected to a magnetic force, with a magnetic flux density inversely proportional to a small parameter $0<\varepsilon\ll 1$, and a nonlinear electric force. To enhance the performance of exponential integrators (EIs), this paper employs a technique that linearizes the ordinary differential equation through a dimension-raising approach. Based on this technique, a new family of EIs is developed that achieves arbitrarily high order. For short-time simulations on the interval $[0,T]$, it is rigorously proved that the proposed method--which employs auxiliary polynomials of degree $k$ and a time step $Δt$--satisfies two distinct error bounds: $O(\varepsilon Δt^{k+1})$ and $O(\varepsilon^{k+2})$. The latter bound guarantees that the algorithm stays accurate even when the step size is of order $O(1)$. Under suitable assumptions, non-negativity of the solution is guaranteed at the continuous level, which is physically relevant since the solution represents a relative concentration. However, this property is not generally preserved at the discrete level, potentially leading to unphysical and unstable numerical approximations. In this work, we analyze a modified version of the Fisher-Kolmogorov model that stabilizes the dynamics around the unstable equilibrium $c=0$. ### [133] [A Damped SWIFT Method for European Option Pricing: Coefficients Decay, Truncation, and Error Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21109)
*Davide Trevisani,José Germán López Salas,Chiheb Ben Hammouda,Cornelis W. Oosterlee*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种阻尼型SWIFT方法（Damped SWIFT）用于欧式期权定价，通过对支付函数施加指数阻尼变换，直接在频域计算傅里叶系数，避免了物理域截断参数。严格分析了不同尾部特征模型下系数的衰减率，给出了高斯型或指数型衰减界，并推导了误差分解与参数选择准则。实验表明该方法在精度、系数数量和稳定性方面均优于原始SWIFT方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始SWIFT方法需要引入物理域截断参数，且依赖于底层密度累积量来确定截断范围，而累积量在实际中往往难以计算或不可得。此外，对于半重尾和重尾模型，原始方法的精度和稳定性存在不足。因此，本文旨在设计一种不依赖累积量、能精确控制截断误差且适用于多种尾部特征模型的傅里叶定价方法。

Method: 对支付函数施加指数阻尼变换，使得傅里叶系数可以直接在频域计算（无需截断参数）。利用奇异点结构（极点、代数分支点、对数分支点）严格分析傅里叶系数的衰减率：轻尾模型得到高斯型衰减界，半重尾和重尾模型得到指数衰减界并附带显式多项式前因子。将误差分解为投影误差、截断误差和求积误差，据此推导阻尼参数、分辨率水平和截断范围的选择规则。

Result: 数值实验表明，Damped SWIFT相比原始SWIFT方法，在相同精度下所需傅里叶系数数量显著减少；在原始方法退化的情况下仍保持稳定；整体定价精度持续提升。

Conclusion: 提出的阻尼型SWIFT方法通过频域直接计算傅里叶系数和严格误差分析，摆脱了对累积量的依赖，实现了对轻尾、半重尾和重尾模型下欧式期权的高效、稳定定价，是一种理论上更完备、实践中更鲁棒的改进方案。

Abstract: We introduce a damped variant of the Shannon Wavelet Inverse Fourier Technique (SWIFT) for pricing European options when the characteristic function of the underlying model is available. The key idea is to apply an exponential damping transformation to the payoff, which enables the direct computation of Fourier coefficients in the frequency domain without introducing an additional physical-domain truncation parameter. We provide a rigorous analysis of the decay of these coefficients by exploiting the singularity structure of the associated Fourier transforms. For light-tailed models, we obtain Gaussian-type decay estimates, while for semi-heavy and heavy-tailed models whose singularities are poles, algebraic branch points, or logarithmic branch points, we derive exponential decay bounds with explicit polynomial prefactors. The resulting sharp bounds make it possible to truncate the Fourier series without relying on the cumulants of the underlying density, which are often unavailable or difficult to compute in practice. We further derive an error decomposition separating projection, truncation, and quadrature errors, and translate the analysis into practical rules for selecting the damping parameter, resolution level, and truncation range. Numerical experiments demonstrate that the proposed approach consistently improves the accuracy of the original SWIFT method while requiring a significantly smaller number of Fourier coefficients and remaining stable in cases where the undamped method deteriorates.

### [134] [A Hyper-Reduced Neural Network-Augmented Semi-smooth Newton Method for Nonlinear Parametric Variational Inequalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21242)

Conclusion: 所提出的神经网络增强降阶框架能有效处理非线性参数化变分不等式，在计算力学中具有实用价值，通过非线性流形近似和超缩减的协同设计，实现了精度与效率的良好平衡。

Abstract: We propose a model order reduction framework for nonlinear parametrized variational inequalities arising in computational mechanics. The high-dimensional model is written in mixed primal-dual form with projection-based complementarity conditions, leading to nonlinear nonsmooth algebraic systems solved by a semi-smooth Newton method in primal-dual form. On this basis, reduced models are constructed by proper orthogonal decomposition (POD) of both primal and dual solution snapshots, and the resulting reduced systems are solved by semi-smooth Newton iterations in the reduced space.
  To address cases where low-dimensional linear spaces provide limited approximation efficiency, we introduce a neural-network-augmented reduced model. Two feedforward networks learn corrections in the truncated POD coordinates of the primal and dual variables, defining a nonlinear manifold approximation that is embedded directly in the semi-smooth Newton iterations. The online cost associated with high-dimensional residual evaluations is reduced through hyper-reduction, using a sparse cubature approach based on greedy nonnegative least squares. Particular attention is paid to the interaction between hyper-reduction and the learned nonlinear manifold.
  The proposed methodology is assessed on two nonlinear variational inequalities with distinct sources of nonlinearity: a two-dimensional obstacle problem with a cubic nonlinearity in the state equation, and a three-dimensional frictional contact problem in which the Coulomb law induces a nonlinear projection in the constraint equation. Numerical results compare the high-dimensional model, the linear reduced model, the neural-network-augmented reduced model, and their hyper-reduced variants, demonstrating accurate approximations with substantial reductions in online computational cost.

### [135] [Adaptive Non-Linear Partition of Unity Methods for Scattered Data Interpolation with Discontinuities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21287)
*Adeeba Haider,Roberto Cavoretto,Juan Ruiz-Álvarez,Dionisio F. Yáñez*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出LOOCV-NL-PUM-GOOI方法，通过局部自适应优化RBF形状参数和补丁半径，在无需先验界面信息的情况下，有效抑制了散乱数据近似中的Gibbs现象，在光滑区域保持精度的同时显著降低间断附近的误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 散乱数据近似中的间断会导致Gibbs现象，严重降低界面附近的精度。现有NL-PUM方法虽能缓解此问题，但其性能高度依赖两个固定超参数（RBF形状参数和补丁半径），缺乏自适应能力。

Method: 采用留一交叉验证（LOOCV）结合全局优化与乐观改进（GOOI）来局部自适应优化两个超参数；核心创新是设计了一个光滑度指标，将感知间断的收缩过程与基于LOOCV的半径选择相联结：光滑区域补丁保持不变，间断附近补丁自动缩小以避免跨越界面。

Result: 在含跳跃间断的合成测试函数以及挪威峡湾高程数据的真实应用中，该方法在间断附近显著降低了近似误差，同时在光滑区域保持了完整精度。

Conclusion: LOOCV-NL-PUM-GOOI无需先验界面几何信息，且不引入超出标准自适应形状参数选择的额外计算成本，是一种高效鲁棒的间断感知散乱数据近似方法。

Abstract: Scattered data approximation with discontinuities is challenging due to the Gibbs phenomenon, which significantly reduces accuracy near interfaces. The recently introduced Non-Linear Partition of Unity Method (NL-PUM) addresses this by combining Radial Basis Function (RBF) interpolation with a non-linear Weighted Essentially Non-Oscillatory (WENO) strategy. While effective, NL-PUM's performance relies heavily on two fixed hyperparameters: the RBF shape parameter and the patch radius. This work extends NL-PUM by adapting both hyperparameters locally using Leave-One-Out Cross-Validation (LOOCV) minimized via Global Optimization with Optimistic Improvement (GOOI). Our main innovation is a smoothness indicator linking a discontinuity-aware shrinkage process to LOOCV-based radius selection: patches in smooth regions remain unchanged, while those near discontinuities automatically shrink to avoid crossing the interface. The resulting method, LOOCV-NL-PUM-GOOI, requires no prior knowledge of interface geometry and introduces no extra cost beyond standard adaptive shape parameter selection. Numerical experiments on synthetic test functions with jump discontinuities and a real-data application to Norwegian Fjords elevation data confirm that this approach substantially reduces approximation error near discontinuities while preserving full accuracy in smooth regions.

### [137] [3D Uncertainty Quantification for the Photo-Acoustic Tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21373)

Method: 提出有限元贝叶斯UQ框架，将随机-优化（RTO）采样策略重写为矩阵自由算法，仅使用前向和伴随波传播生成独立后验样本；构造与离散正向算子精确转置且与连续PAT伴随一致的时间离散化方案，解决伴随一致性问题；研究时间离散化、人工边界条件等因素对后验不确定性的影响。

Abstract: Photoacoustic tomography (PAT) is a promising modality for high-resolution biomedical imaging, motivating the need for reliable uncertainty quantification (UQ) of reconstructed images. Bayesian approaches provide a rigorous framework for UQ but remain computationally challenging for realistic three-dimensional PAT and are sensitive to numerical approximations in the governing wave equation. We develop a finite-element Bayesian UQ framework for PAT that accommodates complex computational domains and detector geometries while enabling large-scale three-dimensional inference. The proposed methodology reformulates the randomize-then-optimize (RTO) sampling strategy as a matrix-free algorithm that generates independent posterior samples using only forward and adjoint wave propagations. Particular attention is given to constructing an adjoint discretization that forms an exact transpose pair with the discrete forward operator while remaining consistent with the continuous PAT adjoint, enabling efficient least-squares solvers within the sampling procedure. We investigate the influence of temporal discretization, artificial boundary conditions, and adjoint consistency on posterior uncertainty and identify discretization strategies that avoid numerical artifacts. The framework is validated against exact posterior statistics, existing Bayesian PAT methods, and Hamiltonian Monte Carlo using the No-U-Turn Sampler (NUTS), and is demonstrated on a three-dimensional problem with approximately $2\times 10^5$ unknowns on a general finite-element domain. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first large-scale Bayesian PAT study on general three-dimensional finite-element geometries, and the methodology extends naturally to a broad class of linear PDE-constrained inverse problems.

### [138] [Jordan algebras, hemiplex numbers, and the Cholesky decomposition of arbitrary symmetric matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21383)
*Alan Edelman,Timothy E. Holy*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为"hemiplex numbers"的非结合代数，将正定矩阵的Cholesky分解推广到任意对称矩阵（包括不定矩阵和奇异矩阵）。该分解无需选主元即可保持带状结构，能参数化零空间并支持近零方向截断，可作为求解对称线性方程组的新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cholesky分解对正定矩阵高效，但不定矩阵的替代方法在数值稳定性和保持带状结构方面面临挑战。本文旨在将Cholesky分解推广到任意对称矩阵，同时保持其无需选主元和保持带状结构的优点。

Method: 通过类比二次方程x^2=c（c≤0）的求解需求，引入一种称为hemiplex numbers的非结合代数，在此基础上定义并推导了适用于任意对称矩阵的Cholesky分解，使其无需选主元即可保持数值稳定性和带状结构。

Result: Hemiplex Cholesky分解对任意对称矩阵均存在且稳定，无需选主元，能保持带状结构；对奇异矩阵可参数化零空间，并支持类似SVD截断的近零方向处理。

Conclusion: 该分解可能成为求解对称线性方程组的一个实用的新工具，弥补了现有方法在处理不定矩阵时的不足。

Abstract: Positive-semidefinite matrices are most efficiently factored using the Cholesky decomposition. For indefinite matrices, the Cholesky factorization does not exist, and the alternatives face greater challenges in achieving numeric stability and preservation of banded structure. Here we pursue an analogy between the requirement for positive-semidefinite matrices and the solution of the quadratic equation x^2 = c for c <= 0. It is shown that a non-associative algebra, called the hemiplex numbers, allows the Cholesky factorization to be computed for arbitrary symmetric matrices. Crucially, the hemiplex Cholesky factorization does not require pivoting for its existence or stability, allowing it to preserve banded structure. For singular matrices it produces a parametrization of the null space, and provides opportunity for truncation of nearly-null directions in a manner similar to common usage of the singular value decomposition. The hemiplex Cholesky factorization may be a practically useful addition to the tools for solving symmetric linear equations.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模糊规则标量目标函数虽然能灵活编码定性偏好和准则间交互，但其诱导的标量偏好景观可能与预期决策语义存在显著差异，现有研究缺乏对这一问题的系统性分析。

Method: 使用两个解析控制的双准则帕累托前沿和一个嵌入的二维占优参考公式，分离前端选择机制与参考改进行为；通过分析隶属度放置、隐式单准则基线规则和显式规则后件来研究标量目标函数的行为。

Result: 表观参考跟踪可能由平坦规则激活平台导致，而真正参考跟踪需要具有低平局模糊性的局部最小值。在占优参考设置中，全局隶属度与竞争后件能恢复鲁棒的帕累托权衡但未必改进每个参考设计；而基于参考的三类规则集能持续改进占优参考、恢复帕累托集并避免平台驱动选择。

Conclusion: 研究提供了诊断指标和实用指南，帮助构建优化行为与预期决策语义一致的模糊标量化函数。

Abstract: Fuzzy-rule-based scalar objective functions provide a flexible way to encode qualitative preferences, reference regions, and interactions between criteria in multi-criteria optimization and decision making. However, the scalar preference landscape induced by such rules can differ substantially from the intended decision semantics. This paper investigates how membership placement, implicit single-criterion baseline rules, and explicit rule consequents affect the behavior of fuzzy scalar objective functions. Two analytically controlled bi-criteria Pareto fronts and an embedded two-dimensional dominated-reference formulation are used to separate front-selection mechanisms from reference improvement behavior. The study shows that apparent reference following can be caused by flat rule-activation plateaus, whereas genuine reference following requires localized minima with low tie ambiguity. In the dominated-reference setting, global memberships with competing consequents recover robust Pareto tradeoffs but do not necessarily improve each reference design. By contrast, a reference-based three-class rule set consistently improves dominated references, recovers the Pareto set, and avoids plateau-driven selection in the present tests. The results provide diagnostic metrics and practical guidance for constructing fuzzy scalarizations whose optimization behavior is consistent with the intended decision semantics.

We analyze its convergence properties and, under stronger conditions, establish finite recovery of the unique solution. Numerical experiments on GAVE and LCP benchmarks illustrate the practical behavior of the framework, including its high final accuracy in the tested settings and its problem-dependent computational tradeoffs.

### [143] [Structure-Preserving Spectral Dynamic Programming on Compact Lie Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20854)
*Shanqing Liu,Yang Qi*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究紧致李群上有限时域最优控制的动态规划半群的谱逼近方法，针对傅里叶方法中L²正交投影与L∞范数下Bellman算子单调非扩张性之间的不匹配问题，提出基于马尔可夫型谱滤波器的离散化方案，在SO(3)上实现正性保持和非扩张性的Fejér型滤波器，并建立了O(√δ+√(ε+1/(δN²)))的收敛率。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态规划半群在紧致李群上的谱逼近面临根本性困难：Bellman算子在L∞范数下单调非扩张，而Peter-Weyl分解的L²正交投影与这一结构不匹配，导致Galerkin迭代中L∞误差被谱投影的Lebesgue常数逐级放大（S¹上对数增长，SO(3)上多项式增长），数值计算中几步内即违反基本界。亟需恢复离散层面的动态规划结构。

Method: 1) 用马尔可夫型谱滤波器替代正交投影；2) 引入辅助热核/消失粘性方案获得Lipschitz数据的L∞收敛性；3) 构造紧致李群上的Fejér型滤波器，具有有限秩、正性保持、非扩张性；4) 基于正体积分的全离散实现，在SO(3)上实现精确Wigner输运。

Result: 对Lipschitz数据建立了收敛率O(√δ+√(ε+1/(δN²)))，粘性可为零，耦合δ=N⁻¹时达到率N^{-1/2}。数值实验验证了预测的收敛率和滤波偏差，量化了两种基于图基线的框架依赖性。

Conclusion: 所提滤波方法有效恢复了离散层面的动态规划结构，无需价值函数先验正则性或粘性意义下的一致性论证，可推广至基于正体积分的全离散实现。

Abstract: We study spectral approximations of the dynamic programming semigroup for finite-horizon optimal control on a connected compact Lie group $G$, and of the associated first-order Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman equation. The Bellman operator is monotone and non-expansive in the supremum norm, while the Peter-Weyl decomposition of $L^{2}(G)$, on which every Fourier method on $G$ rests, is orthogonal, and the mismatch is quantitative. The natural sup-norm error recursion of the Galerkin iteration is amplified at every step by the Lebesgue constant of the spectral projection, which grows logarithmically on $S^{1}$ and polynomially on compact Lie groups of rank one, including $\mathrm{SO}(3)$, and in computation the iteration violates elementary bounds within a few steps. We restore the dynamic programming structure at the discrete level by replacing the orthogonal projection with spectral filters of Markov type. An auxiliary heat-kernel/vanishing-viscosity scheme yields qualitative sup-norm convergence for Lipschitz data. The main result is a Fejér-type filter on $G$, finite-rank, positivity preserving and non-expansive, together with a convergence theorem at the rate $O(\sqrtδ+\sqrt{ε+1/(δN^2)})$ for Lipschitz data, where $δ$ is the time step, $N$ the spectral resolution and $ε$ the viscosity. The viscosity may be zero, and the coupling $δ=N^{-1}$ then gives the rate $N^{-1/2}$. The proof interprets the filter as a small random perturbation of the controlled dynamics, requires neither a priori regularity of the value function nor a consistency argument in the viscosity sense for the filtering step, and extends to a fully discrete realization based on positive cubature, with exact Wigner transport on $\mathrm{SO}(3)$. Numerical experiments confirm the predicted rates and filter bias and quantify the frame dependence of two chart-based baselines.

</details>

*Benjamin Grimmer,Alex L. Wang*

TL;DR: 本文研究一阶凸优化算法的收敛性证明，发现任何保证原始目标间隙上界的一阶方法，在温和条件下也隐含地保证了相同速率的显式原始-对偶间隙，并揭示了对偶证书在动量方法辅助序列中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于性能估计问题（PEP）的工作表明，固定步长一阶方法通常存在结构化的严格收敛证明。本文进一步探究这些证明背后的普适性结构，特别是探索原始间隙保证与对偶证书之间的内在联系。

Method: 从理论上分析一般固定步长一阶方法（包括非光滑Lipschitz问题和光滑问题），利用性能估计问题（PEP）框架，证明在原始目标间隙有界保证的条件下，存在同等收敛速率的显式可计算的原始-对偶间隙，该对偶证书以仿射下界形式呈现。

Result: 证明了任何保证原始目标间隙上界的一阶方法，在温和条件下必然具有一个更强的显式原始-对偶间隙保证，且收敛速率相同。这些隐式最优对偶证书以仿射下界形式存在，并揭示了动量方法中辅助序列的理论作用。

Conclusion: 该工作为一阶凸优化方法的收敛性分析提供了更深刻的理论视角，表明原始间隙保证本质上蕴含了对偶证书的存在，这对理解动量方法的收敛机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: This work considers the design of first-order convex optimization algorithms and convergence proofs. In particular, we consider nonsmooth Lipschitz and smooth problems accessed through a subgradient or gradient oracle, respectively. For the general class of fixed-step first-order methods, prior work on Performance Estimation Problems (PEPs) has shown that structured, tight convergence proofs typically exist. Under mild conditions, we further show that any first-order method guaranteeing a bound on the primal objective gap $f(x_N)-f(x_\star)$ assuming only a bound on $\|x_0-x_\star\|$ actually has a stronger guarantee on an explicit, computable primal-dual gap at the same rate. These implicit optimal dual certificates, which take the form of affine lower bounds, also provide insight into the role of auxiliary sequences in momentum methods.

### [145] [Learning to recover: Adaptive local branching with reinforcement learning for log-truck routing and scheduling under disruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20901)
*Abdelhakim Abdellaoui,Issmail El Hallaoui,Loubna Benabbou,François Aubé,Mouloud Amazouz*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将恢复问题建模为以ℓ1距离（偏差界k）参数化的邻域受限混合整数线性规划序列；精确计算最小可行k值以锚定搜索起点；采用REINFORCE策略梯度算法训练强化学习策略，利用求解器反馈自适应选择后续k值，集中计算资源于有希望的区域，在改进可能性低时终止探索。

Result: 在源自加拿大林业合作伙伴历史数据的周实例上，覆盖所有考虑的中断类别，该方法比固定k值网格搜索和对分搜索基线用更少的求解器调用获得更丰富的帕累托前沿，并在所有配置和中断类型下均能在操作可接受的重优化时间内生成可行恢复方案。

Abstract: We consider the real-time reoptimisation of log-truck routing and scheduling in the Canadian forestry industry following unforeseen disruptions. Road closures, vehicle breakdowns, travel delays, and demand fluctuations invalidate pre-established tactical plans and call for recovery decisions that simultaneously restore feasibility and limit deviation from the original schedule, two objectives inherently in tension under tight time constraints. We formulate recovery as a sequence of neighbourhood-restricted mixed-integer linear programs parameterised by a deviation bound $k$, the $\ell_1$ distance between the recovered and baseline plans. We show that the minimum feasible value $k_{\min}$ can be computed exactly, anchoring the search at its most stable extreme. Rather than targeting a single $k$, we seek a Pareto front of non-dominated recovery plans spanning the stability--cost space, giving dispatchers a structured set of operational options. To navigate this space efficiently, we propose a reinforcement learning policy, trained with the REINFORCE policy-gradient algorithm, that adaptively selects successive values of $k$ from solver feedback, concentrating computational effort in productive regions and terminating exploration when further improvement is unlikely. Evaluated on weekly instances derived from historical data of a Canadian forestry partner, under disruption scenarios covering all event categories considered, the approach recovers richer Pareto fronts with fewer solver calls than fixed-$k$ grid and dichotomic search baselines, and produces feasible recovery plans within operationally acceptable reoptimization times across all configurations and disruption types.

This framework is applied to a realistic hydrogen transport model to evaluate periodic operating regimes under periodic fluctuations in supply and demand.

Abstract: AI product launches require service-capacity decisions before sufficient product-specific workload histories are available. Early service observations update beliefs about remaining workload, but workload does not physically deplete capacity as inventory demand does. Preserving rapid-response capability may also require costly capacity-access and operational arrangements. We study how a firm should jointly decide current capacity deployment and future response readiness. We formulate a finite-horizon dynamic program with workload beliefs, serviceable capacity, and an absorbing response-channel state. A preservation-deployment decomposition solves one deployment problem for each continuation choice and compares the resulting optimized values. This structure identifies when response readiness should be preserved and how much capacity should be deployed. We operationalize the framework through the Cold-Start Belief Actionability Policy (CBAP), which estimates side-specific values using workload scenarios drawn from predictive beliefs. The results distinguish forecast informativeness from operational actionability and show that current deployment and future response readiness are separate decision margins. Zero deployment may represent Standby rather than Exit, while positive deployment need not imply preserving the response channel.

Method: 1) 定义Goldstein二阶δ-次微分作为广义Hessian矩阵；2) 提出(ε₁,ε₂,δ)-二阶平稳点概念；3) 设计基于三次正则化、高斯平滑和同伦策略的零阶算法；4) 在目标函数满足温和强制型假设下进行迭代复杂度分析。

Result: 成功推导了所提零阶算法在找到近似二阶平稳点时的迭代复杂度上界，该复杂度依赖于目标函数的强制型假设条件。

Conclusion: 该工作为处理具有局部Lipschitz梯度的非凸优化问题提供了新的理论工具和实用的零阶算法框架，在理论上推广了传统二阶优化方法到更广泛的函数类上。

Abstract: We introduce a new generalized Hessian, called the Goldstein second-order $δ$-subdifferential, and an associated notion of $(ε_1,ε_2,δ)$-second-order stationary point for continuously differentiable functions with locally Lipschitz gradients. We propose a zeroth-order algorithm based on cubic regularization and Gaussian smoothing with homotopy to find such approximate second-order stationary points for Lipschitz differentiable functions, and derive the iteration complexity under a mild coercivity-type assumption on the objective function.

</details>

### [154] [Climate-resilient electric vehicle charging infrastructure for sustainable cities: An interpretable causal-ensemble framework for preventive maintenance and low-carbon mobility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21444)
*Cande Lian,Wentao Zeng,Jiabin Wu,Yiming Bie,Wei Zhou*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出FGDSE，一种特征驱动的动态堆叠集成方法，用于预测电动汽车充电设备在多周（1-30天）内的故障风险。该方法将异构信号划分为四个特征族并分配领域专家模型，结合两个深度时序专家处理短期脉冲与长期退化，通过基于时间跨度的门控机制自适应加权集成。基于25个月13个站点数据，FGDSE在10天以上预测窗口超越12个基线，30天时保持约85%宏召回率且AUC仅下降3.2点，并揭示故障主导因素从历史记录转向气候胁迫。SHAP和X-learner提供因果决策支持，识别极端高温为唯一随时间因果效应放大的暴露因素，约30%站点为热敏感型，为气候适应性维护提供量化阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: FGDSE包含四个组件：①将异构信号划分为四个特征族，分别匹配具备相应归纳偏置的领域专家模型；②加入两个深度时序专家（短期脉冲与长期退化）；③采用基于预测时间跨度的门控机制学习自适应权重，动态集成多专家输出，实现1-30天逐日故障风险预测；④结合SHAP归因和X-learner将概率输出扩展为后处理效应下的因果决策支持。

Result: 在25个月13个站点的数据上：①FGDSE在10天以上预测窗口超越12个基线模型；②30天时宏召回率约85%，AUC仅衰减3.2点；③故障主导因素从历史故障记录转向气候胁迫；④极端高温是唯一因果效应随时间放大的暴露因素，约30%站点被识别为热敏感型。

Conclusion: FGDSE为气候韧性充电资产管理提供了可解释的决策支持系统，证明了从反应式维修转向面向气候适应性的预测性维护的可行性，为强化城市交通韧性、支撑低碳出行提供了量化管理阈值。

Abstract: Reliable electric vehicle (EV) charging infrastructure is a cornerstone of sustainable, low-carbon cities, yet urban climate stress such as extreme heat, heavy precipitation, and humidity increasingly raises equipment fault risk and undermines the resilience of urban energy and mobility services. Shifting operation from reactive repair to preventive maintenance depends on accurate, forward-looking fault-risk prediction, a task complicated by the heterogeneous time scales of physical, behavioral, contextual, and historical signals and by forecasting over a multi-week horizon. We develop FGDSE, a feature-governed dynamic stacking ensemble that forms an interpretable decision-support system for climate-resilient charging-asset management. It partitions heterogeneous signals into four feature families, assigns each to a domain expert whose inductive bias matches the data, and adds two deep temporal experts for short-term pulses and long-term degradation; a horizon-wise gating mechanism then learns adaptive weights to forecast daily fault risk over 1 to 30 days. SHAP attribution and an X-learner extend the probabilistic output into causal decision support with post-level treatment effects. On 25 months of data from 13 stations, FGDSE surpasses twelve baselines beyond the ten-day horizon, sustains about 85% macro-recall at 30 days with an AUC decay of only 3.2 points, and reveals a shift of dominance from fault history toward climate stress. It identifies extreme heat as the sole exposure whose causal effect amplifies over time, flagging roughly 30% of posts as heat-sensitive and yielding quantitative thresholds for climate-adaptive maintenance that strengthens urban mobility resilience and sustains low-carbon travel.

### [156] [Barzilai-Borwein Fails Superlinear Convergence on an Open Set of Quadratics for Every Dimension $n\geq 4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21579)
*Dawei Li,Xiaotian Jiang,Mingyi Hong*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文证明Barzilai-Borwein (BB1)方法在严格凸二次规划问题中，对于维度n≥4的情形，存在一个非空开集（正Lebesgue测度）的问题和初始点，使得BB1方法收敛但无法达到根超线性收敛。通过构造一个非共振吸引七周期轨道，证明梯度范数和误差能量范数被几何序列上下界约束，排除了超线性收敛的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: BB方法在实际优化中表现优异，但其收敛动力学特性尚未被充分理解。一个核心未解问题是：BB方法是否对几乎所有严格凸二次问题及初始化都能实现超线性收敛。本文旨在回答这一开放性问题。

Method: 采用计算机辅助证明方法，在四维空间中构造了投影化BB动力学的一个非共振吸引七周期轨道。通过设置显式常数ρ_min=10^{-6}, ρ_max=0.61，构建了维度n≥4的严格凸二次问题族及初始点，使得梯度每个谱分量都被对应的几何序列上下界约束。

Result: 对于每个有限维度n≥4，存在非空开集（正Lebesgue测度）的严格凸二次问题和初始点，使得BB1方法收敛但无法根超线性收敛。梯度范数和能量误差范数满足双向几何估计（相同速率），目标间隙满足平方速率的对应估计。三个量都被几何序列下界约束，排除了超线性收敛。

Conclusion: 对BB方法能否几乎处处超线性收敛这一核心问题给出了否定答案，揭示了BB方法收敛动力学的复杂性，为理解该类方法的收敛性质提供了重要理论界限。

Abstract: Barzilai--Borwein (BB) method has shown strong practical performance in continuous optimization, yet its convergence dynamics remains poorly understood. In particular, a central unresolved question is whether BB converges superlinearly for almost every strictly convex quadratic problem and initialization. We provide a negative answer to this question. Specifically, for every finite dimension $n\geq4$, we construct a nonempty open, hence positive-Lebesgue-measure, family of strictly convex quadratic problems and initial points for which the long Barzilai--Borwein method (BB1) converges but cannot converge root-superlinearly. More precisely, with the explicit constants $ρ_{\min}=10^{-6},ρ_{\max}=0.61$, every spectral component of the gradient is bounded above and below by the corresponding geometric sequence. Consequently, the gradient norm and the energy norm of the error satisfy two-sided geometric estimates with the same rates, while the objective gap satisfies the corresponding estimates with squared rates. In particular, all three quantities are bounded below by geometric sequences, ruling out superlinear convergence. The construction is highly nontrivial, based on a computer-assisted proof of a nonresonant, attracting seven-cycle of the projectivized BB dynamics in dimension four.

</details>

### [157] [Several counterexamples to kinetic Schauder estimates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20682)
*Hongjie Dong,Weinan Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this paper, we construct counterexamples to the Schauder estimate for kinetic Fokker--Planck equations, disproving \cite[Conjecture~1.3]{HW}. The conjectured estimate would control second velocity derivatives using only velocity Hölder regularity of the coefficients and forcing, with no spatial regularity. We also give a zero-forcing variant, where the same {conditions are imposed on} a bounded zeroth-order coefficient. Finally, in dimensions $d\geq 2$, we give endpoint examples showing that bounded velocity-independent forcing may produce bounded distributional stationary solutions whose second velocity derivatives are not locally bounded.

### [158] [On the Spatially Homogeneous Boltzmann Equation with Mass Exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20684)
*Siwei Luo,Jian-Guo Liu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究带有连续质量交换的玻尔兹曼方程，对Grad截断硬势碰撞核，证明了全局弱解的存在性、能量耗散/守恒、高阶矩传播、唯一性，并提出了一种无需细致平衡或相对熵的二阶段自举方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典玻尔兹曼方程通常假设粒子质量不变，而现实中许多系统（如气溶胶、聚合物、颗粒流）存在质量交换过程。作者旨在建立此类方程在硬势Grad截断条件下的全局适定性理论，克服质量浓度在m=0处奇点带来的紧致性困难。

Method: 提出两阶段自举法：第一阶段排除质量集中在m=0的现象；第二阶段将这一控制与碰撞几何相结合，建立一致可积性。该方法无需精细平衡或相对熵结构，适用于有界连续对称交换率和线性增长交换率。

Result: (1) 有界连续对称交换率下，对有限数、质量和动能初值存在全局L1弱解；(2) 高阶矩(1+δ)在有限时间内传播；(3) 在1+γ矩假设下解唯一；(4) 对线性增长交换率建立了局部Hp理论。

Conclusion: 首次在无需详细平衡或相对熵的条件下，建立了带连续质量交换的玻尔兹曼方程的全局适定性，方法具有普适性，为后续研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: We study the spatially homogeneous Boltzmann equation with continuous mass exchange on $X=(0,\infty)_m\times\mathbb R^d_v$, with a Grad cut-off hard-potential collision kernel. For bounded continuous symmetric mass-exchange rates, every nonnegative initial datum with finite number, mass, and kinetic energy admits a global nonnegative $L^1$-integral weak solution in $W^{1,\infty}(0,\infty;L^1(X))$ with number and mass conserved, kinetic energy dissipated. If $\int_X (m|v|^2)^{1+δ} f_0(x)dx<\infty,$ for some $δ>0$, this higher-energy moment propagates on every finite time interval and kinetic energy is conserved through the constructed solution. Moreover, every energy-dissipating solution propagates any such moment. Under the additional $1+γ$ moment assumption, the solution is unique among all energy-dissipating $L^1$-integral weak solutions with the same initial datum. We also establish a local theory for a linearly growing mass-exchange rate. With $H_p(f)=\int_X (1+m+m|v|^2)^pfdx,$ every datum with $H_p(f_0)<\infty$, where $p\ge1+γ$ admits a conservative local $H_p$-solution. Moreover, an $H_p$-solution continues across every finite time $T$ for which $H_{1+γ}(f)\in L^1(0,T).$ This proof requires no detailed-balance or relative-entropy structures. It is based on a new two-stage bootstrap method. The first stage rules out mass concentration at $m=0$, while the second stage combines this control with collision geometry to establish uniform integrability. These estimates provide the compactness needed for the global solution and for the identification of the nonlinear collision form.

</details>


### [159] [Quasilinear equations with exponential growth for Hörmander $q$-sub-Laplacians on stratified Lie groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20685)
*Jesus A. León Tordecilla,Duván Cardona*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文在任意分层李群上证明了具指数非线性项的拟线性方程（水平q-拉普拉斯算子）正弱解的存在性，其中非线性项结合了凹项与指数增长项（可次临界、临界或超临界）。通过证明Lorentz空间中的Trudinger-Moser不等式，并设计Galerkin方法，克服了变分框架缺失的困难，将结果推广到完整范围q∈(1,∞)，涵盖了Rn和Heisenberg群上的已知结论，并讨论了Engel群等特例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在分层李群上研究具指数非线性项的q-次拉普拉斯方程的正解存在性，填补了该领域在完整q取值范围内的理论空白，特别是将先前仅在Rn和Heisenberg群（特定q值）上的结果推广到一般分层李群和任意q∈(1,∞)。

Method: 1. 证明Lorentz空间上的Trudinger-Moser不等式；2. 采用精心设计的Galerkin方法，绕过经典变分法和临界点理论在自然能量空间中不适用的困难；3. 将问题转化为半线性方程后求解正弱解。

Result: 1. 获得了任意分层李群上水平q-拉普拉斯方程正弱解的存在性；2. 将结果推广到完整范围q∈(1,∞)；3. 恢复了Rn上的已知结果，扩展了Heisenberg群上仅对q=2n+2的结论；4. 讨论了Engel群等特例。

Conclusion: 通过结合Lorentz空间Trudinger-Moser不等式与Galerkin方法，成功建立了分层李群上具指数非线性项的q-次拉普拉斯方程正解存在性的统一理论框架，覆盖了完整的q取值范围和多种指数增长类型，为相关领域提供了更一般的数学基础。

Abstract: We prove the existence of positive weak solutions for a quasilinear equation with exponential nonlinearity on arbitrary stratified Lie groups for \emph{horizontal $q$-Laplacians,} also called $q$-sub-Laplacians on these groups. The nonlinearity combines a concave term with an exponential growth that can be subcritical, critical, or supercritical with respect to the Trudinger--Moser inequality for Lorentz spaces on stratified Lie groups. We prove a version of this inequality in this paper. Since the problem is not variational in the natural energy space, classical minimisation or critical-point techniques do not apply directly. Positive solutions to the resulting semilinear equation are then obtained via a carefully designed Galerkin method applied to this setting. Our main theorem recovers previous known results on $\mathbb{R}^n$ in the complete range $q\in (1,\infty),$ and the previous known result on the Heisenberg group $\mathbb{H}^n$ for $q=2n+2,$ and is extended here in the full range $q\in (1,\infty)$. Other particular and fundamental cases, including the Engel group, are discussed.

</details>


### [160] [Pointwise mean-value formulas with quantitative remainder for higher-order Poisson equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20776)

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文为高阶泊松方程（含非零强迫项）的解引入了一族基于迭代均值线性组合的均值公式，并给出了由强迫项振荡量化的精确余项。同时证明了正则性结果及均值性质的强逆命题：仅局部可积的函数若满足该均值公式，则必为高阶泊松方程的正则解，且正则性由强迫项决定。这些结果共同给出了高阶泊松方程解的均值刻画。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构造迭代均值的线性组合，引入一族均值公式。利用强迫项的振荡量量化余项，并基于该公式建立局部可积函数到正则解的正则性提升论证。

Abstract: Higher-order Poisson equations involve an integer power of the Laplacian and a nonzero forcing term, and appear in areas of physics and engineering such as hydrodynamics, structural engineering, and image processing. We introduce a family of mean-value formulas for solutions to higher-order Poisson equations, given in terms of linear combinations of iterated means, with an exact remainder quantified by the oscillation of the forcing term. We also prove a regularity result and a strong converse to the mean-value property, in the sense that merely locally integrable functions satisfying our formulas are regular solutions of the higher-order Poisson equation. In contrast with the homogeneous case, where the mean-value property forces smoothness, the regularity attainable here is dictated by the regularity of the forcing term. ### [166] [An inverse coefficient problem for a semilinear wave equation by the first order linearization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20949)

  <summary>Details</summary>

We demonstrate that the unknown coefficient \(q\) appearing in the semilinear wave equation \(\square u + q u^m = 0\) with Neumann boundary conditions can be reconstructed with Hölder stability from the linearized Neumann-to-Dirichlet (NtD) map. Our approach combines first-order linearization with the Principle of Inclusion-Exclusion (PIE) identity, and employs geometric optics solutions for wave equations in two distinct regimes: the case \(m=2\) with \(q = q(x)\), and the case \(m \ge 3\) with \(q = q(t,x)\).   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献在各向异性拟线性椭圆方程（临界指数p=N）的刚性理论方面存在空白，尤其是在非线性边界条件下，缺乏对弱解刚性的充分刻画。本文旨在填补这一空白，在更弱的假设下建立刚性结果。

Method: 利用各向异性算子a(ξ)=H^{N-1}(ξ)∇H(ξ)的结构，推导了一个涉及各向异性梯度和边界第二基本形式的关键积分不等式，作为核心技术工具。在非线性的自然单调性假设下，结合该不等式进行弱解分析。

Abstract: This paper is devoted to the rigidity of weak solutions for anisotropic $N$-Laplacian equations with Neumann or Robin boundary conditions on smooth bounded convex domains of $\mathbb{R}^N$. The anisotropic operator is given by $$a(ξ) = H^{N-1}(ξ)\nabla H(ξ),$$ where $H$ stands for a norm on $\mathbb{R}^N$; this formulation contains the classical $N$-Laplacian as a special case. We establish a key integral inequality involving the anisotropic gradient and the second fundamental form of the domain boundary, which acts as the core technical tool in our proofs. Under natural monotonicity assumptions on the nonlinearity, we prove that all weak solutions to the Neumann boundary problem are constant, without requiring any a priori boundedness assumption on the solution. Furthermore, we extend this rigidity result to Robin boundary value problems by imposing suitable constraints on the boundary nonlinear term. Moreover, our rigidity results remain valid not only on bounded convex domains but also on suitable unbounded domains. By working under substantially weaker assumptions than those previously available, we establish rigidity results that fill the gaps in the existing literature for anisotropic $N$-Laplacian equations with nonlinear boundary conditions and substantially extend the rigidity theory of anisotropic quasilinear elliptic equations at the critical exponent $p=N$.

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于贝叶斯优化的三维逆散射框架，用于从单次入射场的远场数据中跟踪刚性运动目标的位置和方向，并在目标形状未知时利用神经网络进行初始识别，数值实验验证了方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决三维空间中利用单次入射场远场数据实时跟踪刚性运动目标的位置和方向这一逆散射问题，扩展此前在二维空间中的研究工作。

Result: 建立了后验一致性的理论保证，并通过数值实验验证了所提出框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的贝叶斯优化框架能够有效跟踪三维刚性运动目标，并能在形状未知时借助神经网络进行初始识别，为实际逆散射跟踪问题提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: We investigate a three-dimensional inverse scattering problem for tracking a rigidly moving target from far-field data generated by a single incident field. Extending our recent two-dimensional study, we develop a Bayesian optimization framework for simultaneously tracking the target's location and orientation over successive time steps, with the translational and rotational motions modeled as independent stochastic processes. We derive analytical formulas for the far-field pattern under translations and rotations and use them to design a Bayesian optimization procedure tailored to the tracking problem. We further establish posterior consistency for the underlying probabilistic model. When the target shape is unknown, its shape is identified at the initial time using a fully connected neural network trained on a precomputed dataset. Numerical experiments validate the effectiveness of the proposed framework.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功构建了行波周期“滚波”解的分支，并证明了在小波数和低雷诺数两种情形下，Orr-Sommerfeld方程的相关假设成立。

Abstract: We construct a branch of travelling periodic `roll wave' solutions to the free-boundary incompressible Navier--Stokes equations on an inclined plane in two dimensions. These solutions bifurcate from a parallel shear flow, under natural assumptions on the related Orr--Sommerfeld equation. Using techniques from analytic global bifurcation theory, we extend the local branch to a global curve of solutions. A key step of the proof is reformulating the problem, including the unknown free boundary, as an elliptic system in the sense of Agmon--Douglis--Nirenberg. Finally, we verify the hypotheses on the Orr--Sommerfeld equation for two regimes: small wavenumber and low Reynolds number.

### [172] [Global existence and boundedness for a degenerate chemotaxis system with indirect signal production via minimizing movement schemes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21211)
*Tatsuya Hosono,Philippe Lauren{\cc}ot*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 建立时间离散方案，第一方程采用2-Wasserstein距离下的梯度流结构，另外两个方程采用L²变分结构；利用流交换方法和离散极大正则性进行证明。

Result: 次临界情形下对任意初始数据证明弱解整体存在且有界；临界和超临界情形下在初始数据满足小性条件时成立。

Abstract: Global existence and boundedness of weak solutions for a fully parabolic degenerate chemotaxis system with indirect signal production are proved for any initial data in the subcritical case and under smallness conditions in the critical and supercritical cases. To construct weak solutions, a time discrete scheme is set up, for which the first equation has a gradient flow structure with respect to the 2-Wasserstein distance, while the other two equations feature an L\textsuperscript{2}-variational structure. The proof relies in particular on the flow interchange method and discrete maximal regularity.

### [173] [Neutral curves and traveling waves in plane Poiseuille flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21265)
*Hui Li,Yuxi Wang,Zhifei Zhang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了高雷诺数下不可压缩平面泊肃叶流的Orr-Sommerfeld算子谱，在Tollmien-Schlichting特征值区域证明了中性曲线下支和上支的存在唯一性，并给出了粘性系数与波数之间的渐近标度律：下支ν~|α|^7，上支ν~|α|^11；等价地，α^2~ν^{2/7}和α^2~ν^{2/11}。同时建立了中性特征值的单性并验证了横向穿越条件。证明基于边界适配的Rayleigh-Airy迭代方案。这些谱结果验证了Joseph-Sattinger和Iooss经典Hopf分支框架所需的假设，从而在平面泊肃叶流的中性点处得到分岔的行波解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为高雷诺数下平面泊肃叶流的中性曲线（下支和上支）提供严格的数学存在唯一性证明，并给出精确的渐近标度律，同时验证Hopf分支理论所需的条件，从而为从层流到行波解的分岔提供严格数学基础。

Method: 采用边界适配的Rayleigh-Airy迭代方案，结合对修正项及其参数导数的精确展开和精细估计，对Orr-Sommerfeld算子谱进行渐近分析。

Result: 证明了中性曲线下支和上支的存在唯一性，给出粘性-波数渐近律：ν~|α|^7（下支）和ν~|α|^11（上支）；建立了中性特征值的单性，验证了横向穿越条件。

Conclusion: 所得谱结果满足了Joseph-Sattinger和Iooss的经典Hopf分支框架所需假设，从而严格保证了在平面泊肃叶流中性点处存在分岔的行波解。

Abstract: We study the spectrum of the Orr--Sommerfeld operator associated with the incompressible plane Poiseuille flow in the high-Reynolds-number regime. In the Tollmien--Schlichting eigenvalue region, we prove the existence and uniqueness of the lower and upper branches of the neutral curve. For each sufficiently small fixed wavenumber $α$, the viscosities corresponding to the lower and upper neutral branches satisfy $ν\sim |α|^7$ and $ν\sim |α|^{11}$, respectively. Equivalently, for each sufficiently small viscosity $ν$, the corresponding lower and upper neutral wavenumbers satisfy $α^2\sim ν^{2/7}$ and $α^2\sim ν^{2/11}$, respectively. We also establish the simplicity of the neutral eigenvalues and verify the transversal crossing condition on both neutral branches. The proof is based on a boundary-adapted version of the Rayleigh--Airy iteration scheme, together with precise expansions and refined estimates for the correction terms and their parameter derivatives. These spectral results verify the assumptions required in the classical Hopf bifurcation framework of Joseph--Sattinger \cite{JS1972} and Iooss \cite{Iooss1972}, and hence yield traveling-wave solutions bifurcating from the plane Poiseuille flow at the neutral points.

</details>


### [174] [An $L^p$-theory for global weak solutions to the Navier-Stokes equations in exterior domains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21282)
*Filippo Palma*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了外区域中Navier-Stokes初边值问题在Lebesgue空间L^p（p∈(2,3)）初始数据下的全局弱解存在性，并给出了结构定理，证明弱解在某一时刻后变得正则且几乎处处时间正则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管局部强/温和解的L^p理论在文献中已很完善，但外区域中全局弱解的相应理论尚属空白，本文旨在填补这一缺失。

Method: 采用L^p空间（p∈(2,3)）的初始数据，针对外区域中的Navier-Stokes初边值问题，建立全局弱解的存在性证明，并推导结构定理。

Result: 证明了外区域中全局弱解的存在性；弱解在某一时刻后变为正则解，且几乎处处时间正则；结果同样适用于Cauchy问题和半空间中的初边值问题。

Conclusion: 本文建立了外区域Navier-Stokes方程在L^p（2<p<3）初始数据下的全局弱解存在性及正则性理论，推广了经典结果。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the Navier-Stokes initial boundary value problem in exterior domains with initial data in the Lebesgue space $L^p$, $p\in (2,3)$, and show the existence of a global weak solution. For the quoted solution, we also furnish a structure theorem. In particular, we see that the weak solution becomes regular after a certain instant of time and it is also regular a. e. in time. Although a general $L^p$-theory for local strong/mild solutions is well-established in the literature, a corresponding theory for global weak solutions in exterior domains seems to be new. Of course, our results hold in the particular cases of the Cauchy problem and the initial boundary value problem in a half-space.

### [175] [Magnetic relaxation for the MHD equations via the stable manifold method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21328)
*Gennaro Ciampa,Renato Lucà*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文证明：对于稳态欧拉方程的任意足够小且正则的解B，存在无穷维的非电阻磁流体力学方程（MHD）的解族(u,b)，这些解随时间指数衰减至(0,B)，即形成平衡态(0,B)附近的稳定流形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非电阻MHD方程是否存在从任意初始状态向稳态欧拉方程解B松弛的全局正则解，并理解这种松弛过程中磁拓扑的保持性。

Method: 通过构造性分析，在平衡态(0,B)附近利用动力系统理论证明稳定流形的存在性，结合小扰动和正则性条件，建立指数衰减到平衡态的无穷维解族。

Result: (1) 存在无穷维MHD解族(u,b)指数衰减至(0,B)；(2) 提供了非电阻MHD方程的一类大范围全局正则解；(3) 证明稳态欧拉方程的解通过MHD dynamics可以被Moffatt意义下拓扑可达，且磁力线拓扑在极限t→+∞时完全保持。

Conclusion: 稳态欧拉方程的小正则解可通过非电阻MHD方程从一大类磁场拓扑可达，磁拓扑在极限过程中完全保持；但该解族是否与真正的稳定流形重合仍是开放问题。

Abstract: We prove that given any sufficiently small and regular solution $B$ of the stationary Euler equations there exists an infinite dimensional family of solutions $(u,b)$ of the non-resistive magnetohydrodynamics equations (MHD) that relax to $(0, B)$. More precisely, $(u,b) \to (0, B)$ exponentially fast as $t \to +\infty$. This family may be viewed as lying in the stable manifold of the non-resistive MHD equations around the equilibrium state $(0, B)$. The problem whether it actually coincides with the stable manifold remains open. As a byproduct of our result, we provide a large class of global regular solutions of the non-resistive MHD equations. Another consequence is that any sufficiently small and regular solution of the stationary Euler equation is (non-trivially) topologically accessible via MHD from a large class of magnetic fields according to the definition of Moffatt and, in this scenario, the topology of the magnetic lines is (entirely) preserved in the limit $t \to + \infty$.

### [176] [Double screening in the training dynamics of variational physics-informed neural networks for heterogeneous coupled parabolic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21352)
*Ali Ouattara Kouma,Gossrin Jean-Marc Bomisso*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文分析了变分物理信息神经网络（VPINN）在线性耦合对流-扩散-反应系统训练中的动力学机制，提出了"双重筛选定理"，揭示了主导对流下系统退化、训练速率下降、条件数增长等关键现象，并证明Adam优化器在适当架构下可缓解训练困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解变分物理信息神经网络在求解耦合对流-扩散-反应系统时的训练动态，特别是当系统存在"异质性"（仅部分分量受对流传输）时，训练困难的根本原因及缓解策略。

Method: 在神经正切核（NTK）框架下，将时空变分残差的梯度流简化为线性微分系统，其算子为由系统算子的时空符号与矩阵切向核构建的Gram矩阵。通过推导Schur补的精确表达式，分析主导对流条件下的系统行为。

Result: 1) 双重筛选定理：主导对流下，Schur补退化为仅含扩散块符号与核Schur补的表达式，无耦合项；2) 筛选耦合能的精确恒等式；3) 训练速率退化律，由核的典型相关性控制；4) 条件数随Péclet数增长的上界；5) 时间频率不参与筛选机制；6) Adam优化器在适当架构下可缓解条件数增长导致的训练困难。

Conclusion: 训练困难主要归因于优化器本身（条件数增长导致共享步长梯度下降变慢），而非近似能力的不足。Adam的自适应缩放可在架构将对流与扩散参数分离时缓解该问题，验证了双重筛选定理给出的架构设计建议。

Abstract: We analyze the training dynamics of variational physics-informed neural networks applied to linear coupled parabolic convection--diffusion--reaction systems, called heterogeneous when only a subset of the components undergoes convective transport. In the neural tangent kernel regime, the gradient flow on the space-time variational residuals reduces to a linear differential system whose operator is a Gram matrix built from the space-time symbol of the system operator and the matrix tangent kernel. The main result is a double screening theorem. Under dominant convection, the Schur complement of this matrix relative to the block of convective components converges to an expression that involves only the diffusive block of the symbol, with no coupling term, together with the Schur complement of the tangent kernel. From this we derive four consequences, namely an exact identity quantifying the screened coupling energy, a degradation law for the training rate governed by the canonical correlations of the kernel, a bound on the condition number in terms of the Péclet number, and the non-participation of temporal frequencies in the screening mechanism. The growth of the condition number slows down shared-step gradient descent, whereas the continuous flow suffers no slowdown, which makes the training difficulty attributable to the optimizer rather than to the approximation. We finally show that the Adam optimizer, through its adaptive scaling, mitigates this difficulty provided that the architecture separates the parameters associated with the convective and diffusive components, confirming the architectural prescription that follows from the second screening. The predictions are validated numerically down to machine precision, on a two-dimensional exchanger, and by the full training of finite-width networks.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先建立非局部项的弱下半连续性以解决良定性并证明极小元存在；然后利用内变分和Danskin型距离函数微分推导驻定性条件，包括变分不等式、正性集上的PDE，以及在非退化假设下的自由边界条件。

Abstract: We study a free boundary problem of minimising a functional containing a non-local term rewarding depth into the zero phase: for $u\ge0$ on a bounded, open set $Ω\subset\mathbb R^d$, we minimise $$J(u) = \int_Ω\left(\frac12|\nabla u|^2 - fu\right) \;-\; \int_{\{u=0\}} F\big(\mathrm{dist}(x,\partial \{u=0\})\big)\;\mathrm{d}x.$$ This kind of functional arises for example from a two-membranes problem with an adhesive contact energy. We first address a well-definedness issue caused by the non-local, boundary-sensitive nature of the functional and prove existence of minimisers, establishing along the way a weak lower semicontinuity result for the non-local term. We then derive stationarity conditions for minimisers, including a variational (Euler--Lagrange type) inequality, a PDE on the positivity set, and, under a mild non-degeneracy assumption, a free boundary condition obtained via inner variations and a Danskin-type differentiation of the distance function.

### [178] [Sharp One-bubble Critical-Point Stability and Global Compactness for the Sobolev Trace Inequality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21429)

Conclusion: 成功将内部区域的单泡临界点稳定性理论推广至边界迹泛函设定，建立了 sharp 的定量稳定性结果，完善了临界迹泛函的分析框架。

Abstract: Let $n\ge3$ and $1<p<n$. We first prove the local trace analogue of the sharp one-bubble critical-point stability theorem of Liu and Zhang~\cite{LiuZhang2025}: near a positive trace-bubble, the Euler--Lagrange residual controls the gradient distance to the normalized trace-bubble manifold with the sharp power $\max\{1,p-1\}$. Then, we establish a Struwe-type compactness theorem for the critical trace functional, which gives the trace counterpart of the Mercuri--Willem decomposition~\cite{MercuriWillem2010}. Combining Struwe-type compactness with the local stability estimate yields a sharp quantitative one-bubble critical-point stability theorem.

Motivation: 理解粘性不可压缩流体中涡量集中在曲线上的演化行为，特别是验证局部感应近似（LIA）下双法向流对涡旋运动的描述在Navier-Stokes框架中的有效性。

Method: 采用Lamb-Oseen型涡旋作为显式主导阶剖面，加上低阶扰动项构造解；通过Morrey $\mathcal{M}^{\infty}$范数控制扰动部分；并将该分析框架应用于Hasimoto孤子解。

Result: 在νt≪1且Γ/ν足够小的条件下，涡量由围绕曲线演化的Lamb-Oseen型涡旋主导；对于Hasimoto孤子，估计关于扭转参数一致，使得在大扭转区域中孤子能够发生宏观位移，并且Navier-Stokes解中与双法向速度相关的动能分布保持集中且发生阶数一的位移。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了粘性流体中涡丝运动的严格数学理论，为LIA近似在不可压Navier-Stokes方程中的有效性提供了数学证明，并展示了Hasimoto孤子在有限时间内的宏观迁移行为。

Abstract: We study the evolution of a viscous incompressible fluid whose initial vorticity is supported on a smooth open curve. We show that, for $νt\ll 1$ and sufficiently small Reynolds number $Γ/ν$, the vorticity is described at leading order by a Lamb--Oseen type vortex concentrated around a curve evolving according to the binormal flow predicted by the localized induction approximation. The solution is written as an explicit leading-order profile plus a lower-order perturbation, which is controlled in a Morrey $\mathcal{M}^{\infty}$ norm.
  Then, we apply this construction to the Hasimoto soliton. In this case, the estimates are uniform with respect to the torsion parameter, allowing us to consider a large-torsion regime in which the soliton undergoes a macroscopic displacement. We show that the corresponding Navier--Stokes solution contains a localized portion of the kinetic-energy distribution, associated with the binormal velocity, which remains concentrated inside a moving physical region and undergoes an order-one displacement during an admissible time interval.

</details>


### [180] [Critical GJMS Equations on $\mathbb{H}^n \times \mathbb{S}^m$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21451)
*Qiaoqiao Hua,Jungang Li,Chunxia Tao*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了双曲-球面乘积流形 $\mathbb{H}^n\times\mathbb{S}^m$ 上带临界指数和吸收项 $\lambda$ 的 GJMS 算子 $P_k$ 方程，给出了在 $0<\lambda<\Lambda_0$ 和阈值 $\lambda=\Lambda_0$ 情形下非平凡弱解的存在性条件，并证明了在严格欧几里得不等式假设下，极小化序列模去轴保持变换后是紧的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双曲-球面乘积流形上研究高阶 GJMS 算子临界方程的可解性及最佳 Sobolev 常数的可达性，特别是阈值情形下 $L^2$ 强制失效时的紧性恢复问题。

Method: 利用欧几里得极值函数局部化建立严格 Sobolev 不等式；在阈值情形采用共紧性分析（cocompactness）结合相对于临界变换的 profile 分解，处理剩余项在 $L^q$ 范数下的渐近消失性质。

Result: 当 $0<\lambda<\Lambda_0$ 且 $S_{\lambda,k}(M)<S_{N,k}$ 时解存在；当 $N\geq4k$ 或 $2k+2\leq N<4k$ 且 $\lambda>\Lambda_{\text{loc}}$ 时不等式成立。阈值情形下若 $S_{\Lambda_0,k}(M)<S_{N,k}$ 则解存在，且极小化序列模去 $\mathcal{A}=\mathbb{R}^{n-1}\times\{0\}$ 轴保持变换后紧。

Conclusion: 建立了双曲-球面乘积流形上 GJMS 算子临界方程解的存在性理论，揭示了阈值情形下紧性缺失仅源于常数球面本征空间，并通过 profile 分解与共紧性方法恢复了模去轴保持变换的紧性。

Abstract: Let $M=\mathbb{H}^n\times\mathbb{S}^m$, where $n\geq 2$, $m\geq 1$, and $N=n+m$. Let $P_k$ be the order-$2k$ GJMS operator, with $1\leq k<N/2$, and assume that $Λ_0=\infσ_{L^2(M)}(P_k)>0$. We study$$P_kU-λU=|U|^{q-2}U,\qquad q=\frac{2N}{N-2k},\qquad 0<λ\leqΛ_0,$$and attainment of the associated critical quotient $S_{λ,k}(M)$.
  Let $S_{N,k}$ be the Euclidean best Sobolev constant. For $0<λ<Λ_0$, the inequality $S_{λ,k}(M)<S_{N,k}$ implies attainment and a nontrivial weak solution. Localized Euclidean extremals establish this inequality when $N\geq4k$, or when $2k+2\leq N<4k$ and $λ>Λ_{\mathrm{loc}}$, where $Λ_{\mathrm{loc}}$ is explicit. If $N\geq2k+2$ and $S_{Λ_0,k}(M)<S_{N,k}$, attainment also holds at $λ=Λ_0$ in the threshold form completion.
  At the threshold, $L^2$-coercivity fails precisely on the constant spherical eigenspace. We combine cocompactness for its hyperbolic coefficient with a profile decomposition relative to the critical transformations preserving $\mathcal{A}=\mathbb{R}^{n-1}\times{0}$. Under the threshold hypotheses above, the strict Euclidean inequality excludes concentration escaping $\mathcal{A}$ from normalized minimizing sequences. If $r_j^{(J)}$ denotes the remainder after the first $J$ extracted profiles, then$$\lim_{J\to\infty}\limsup_{j\to\infty}|r_j^{(J)}|_{L^q(\mathbb{R}^N)}=0,$$which yields compactness modulo the axis-preserving transformations.

</details>


### [181] [Eigenfunctions, free boundaries, and time-frequency localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21590)
*João P. G. Ramos*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文为时频局部化算子建立了逆理论，核心思想是自由边界问题：从给定的谱数据恢复未知的局部化域边界。主要结果包括：1）构造了多项式逼近高斯时的实解析局部化域；2）恢复了Abreu-Dörfler关于Hermite多项式局部化域为圆盘的刻画；3）证明了Gómez-Guerra-Ramos-Tilli稳定性不等式指数1/2的最优性；4）证明了高斯Faber-Krahn问题的局部极大值点为圆盘，并给出了Nicola-Tilli定理的新证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时频分析中，局部化算子的正问题（给定域求谱）已被充分研究，但逆问题（给定谱数据求域）尚未有一般性理论。本文旨在建立时频局部化算子的逆理论框架，填补这一空白。

Method: 将逆问题转化为自由边界问题，利用特征函数作为几何数据来确定局部化域。结合变分原理、Fock空间集中紧致性剖面分解等工具，建立了从谱数据恢复局部化域的一般方法。

Result: 1) 构造了多项式逼近高斯时的实解析局部化域（首个一般性逆构造）；2) 恢复了Abreu-Dörfler关于圆盘为Hermite多项式唯一局部化域的刻画；3) 证明了稳定性不等式指数1/2的最优性；4) 证明了高斯Faber-Krahn问题局部极大值点为圆盘，并给出了Nicola-Tilli定理的新证明。

Conclusion: 建立了时频局部化算子逆理论的一般框架，展示了自由边界方法在时频分析中的强大威力，并为相关领域（如稳定性不等式、Faber-Krahn问题）提供了新的洞见和结果。

Abstract: We develop an inverse theory for time-frequency localization operators, whose central idea that of is free-boundary problem: the localization domain is unknown and its boundary is recovered from prescribed spectral data. The approach is based on the principle that an eigenfunction may be regarded as geometric data which determines a localization domain, and prescribing it has strong consequences for the associated variational problem.
  Four main results follow from this main framework. First, if $f_0$ is a polynomial sufficiently close to the Gaussian and $λ\in(0,1)$, we construct a real-analytic domain $U_λ$ such that $f_0$ is an eigenfunction of the localization operator associated with $U_λ$ and with eigenvalue $λ$, giving a general inverse construction of localization domains, which is the first in the literature. Second, we recover the null-set invariant Abreu-Dörfler characterization of disks as the only localization domains of Hermite polynomials in the simply connected case. Third, we prove optimality of the exponent $1/2$ in the Gómez-Guerra-Ramos-Tilli quantitative stability inequality, answering thus a question posed by those authors. Finally, we show that local maximizers of the Gaussian Faber-Krahn problem are disks, which extends the Nicola-Tilli concentration inequality to the local case as well, and, as a matter of fact, as a consequence of a Fock space concentration-compactness profile decomposition, we are able to use this to give a new, different proof of the Nicola-Tilli theorem.

</details>

### [182] [Group Chunks in Model Theory and Algebraic Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20824)
*Ronan O'Gorman*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文在层论框架下建立了群块定理，并发展了Hrushovski方法在代数几何中的类比，利用Hilbert方案替代模型论工具，将结果推广到更一般的基概形上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将模型论中的群块定理推广到更一般的范畴论和代数几何语境，突破原有结果对特定基概形的限制。

Method: (1) 在任意范畴中研究部分态射，证明部分岩浆预层到群的普遍态射存在性；(2) 利用Hilbert方案研究"典范"有理态射族；(3) 在模型论侧将$M^{eq}$中的类型可定义集解释为类型可定义集的层商；(4) 在代数几何侧发展任意基概形上的有理态射及其族理论。

Result: 建立了站点上层论的群块定理；将Hrushovski的群块构造方法从模型论移植到代数几何，并推广到更一般的基概形上。

Conclusion: 通过范畴论和层论工具统一了模型论与代数几何中的群块构造，为跨领域应用提供了技术基础。

Abstract: We formulate a group chunk theorem in the context of sheaves on sites which generalizes many similar results in model theory and algebraic geometry. Secondly, we develop an algebro-geometric analogue of Hrushovski's method of producing a group chunk from germs of definable functions on stationary types. The use of the model-theoretic tools of canonical bases and elimination of imaginaries is replaced with the use of Hilbert schemes to study ``canonical'' families of rational morphisms, allowing us to extend the previously known results over more general base schemes.
  The proofs of these results involve some technical work which may be of independent interest. First, we study partial morphisms in arbitrary categories, and show that a presheaf of partial magmas on a small category admits a universal morphism to a group. On the model theory side, we show that type-definable sets of $M^{eq}$ can be interpreted as sheaf quotients of type-definable sets. On the algebraic geometry side, we develop a theory of rational morphisms and families of rational morphisms of schemes over an arbitrary base.

### [183] [Prescribed extension spectra of mock automorphisms over finite fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20829)
*Stefan Barańczuk,Tomasz Ślusarski*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限域上显式模拟自同构族的有限扩张置换谱，证明了每个有限非空除数闭子集都会出现，从而反驳了Maubach-Willems猜想；同时给出了满足特定雅可比条件的映射的总度下界，并构造了达到该下界的映射，还确定了单变量模拟自同构的最小次数表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反驳Maubach和Willems关于每个模拟自同构置换无限多个有限扩张的猜想，并研究有限域上模拟自同构的置换谱与次数下界问题。

Method: 通过分类有限扩张置换谱、构造满足雅可比条件的映射、分析一维情况下的谱与次数界、利用约化置换多项式等工具进行构造与证明。

Result: 每个有限非空除数闭子集均可作为置换谱出现；满足Jac(F)=I_n且F|_{\F_q^n}=id的映射总度至少为p(q+1)，且对n≥2该界可由谱为{1}的映射达到；一维情形下奇域和F_2上达到相同界，偶域q>2给出了非例外构造；单变量非例外模拟自同构的最小次数μ_p满足μ_2=6, μ_3=12, μ_p=pδ_p(p≥5)。

Conclusion: Maubach-Willems猜想不成立；给出了模拟自同构置换谱的完整分类及次数下界；所有非平凡反例的几何一般次数均可被p整除。

Abstract: We classify the finite-extension permutation spectra occurring in an explicit family of mock automorphisms over finite fields. Every finite nonempty divisor-closed subset of $\N_{>0}$ occurs; in particular, this disproves Maubach and Willems conjecture that every mock automorphism permutes infinitely many finite extensions.
  Every finite-spectrum map satisfying \[
  \Jac(F)=I_n,\qquad F|_{\F_q^n}=\id \] has total degree at least $p(q+1)$. For every $n\geq2$, this bound is attained by a map with spectrum $\{1\}$. In dimension one, the same bound and exact spectrum $\{1\}$ are attained over every odd field and over $\F_2$; for even $q>2$ we give a nonexceptional construction with an effective finite bound for its spectrum. If $δ_p$ denotes the least degree of a nonlinear reduced permutation polynomial over $\mathbb F_p$, then the least degree $μ_p$ of a nonexceptional one-variable mock automorphism satisfies \[ μ_2=6,\qquad μ_3=12,\qquad μ_p=pδ_p\quad(p\ge5). \] We also record a cofinite-spectrum criterion and isolate the surviving prime-to-$p$ question. Every nontrivial counterexample constructed here has geometric generic degree divisible by $p$.

</details>

Conclusion: 半正定adelic线丛的绝对最小值不一定能被代数点达到，这一发现深化了对adelic线丛算术性质的理解。

Abstract: There exists a semipositive adelic line bundle on a projective variety over $\mathbb{Q}$ whose absolute minimum does not attain the minimum by algebraic points. The construction is based on arithmetic properties of a family of dynamical systems over $\mathbb{P}^1$.

### [185] [An Explicit Characteristic-$2$ Counterexample to the Separable Jacobian Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20968)
*Irit Huq-Kuruvilla*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文在特征为2的域上构造了一个三维仿射空间上的多项式自同态，其雅可比行列式恒为1，有理函数域扩张次数为3，但该映射非单射。由于2≠3，这构成了对通常的Adjamagbo（或可分形式）雅可比猜想在特征2下的反例，并通过稳定化方法推广到所有n≥3维。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 雅可比猜想在特征零域上断言：若多项式映射的雅可比行列式为非零常数，则该映射具有多项式逆。该猜想在正特征下的相应表述（Adjamagbo形式）长期未决，本文旨在构造特征2下的反例，揭示该设定下猜想的失效。

Method: 在特征2的域k上，显式构造一个三次多项式自同态F: A³→A³，使其雅可比行列式恒为1，但映射非单射。通过计算有理函数域扩张次数为3（与特征2互质），验证其符合Adjamagbo形式条件却仍非单射。进一步利用稳定化技巧将反例提升到任意维数n≥3。

Result: 成功构造出满足雅可比行列式为1、域扩张次数为3的非单射多项式自同态，证明在特征2下Adjamagbo形式的雅可比猜想不成立，并将反例推广至所有n≥3维。

Conclusion: 特征2情形下，雅可比猜想的可分形式（Adjamagbo形式）不成立，揭示了正特征与特征零情形之间的本质差异，并为后续研究雅可比猜想在不同特征下的成立条件提供了重要反例。

Abstract: Let $k$ be a field of characteristic $2$. We exhibit an explicit polynomial endomorphism $F: \mathbb{A}_k^3\to\mathbb{A}_k^3$ whose Jacobian determinant is identically $1$, whose induced extension of rational function fields has degree $3$, and which is nevertheless noninjective. Since $2\neq 3$, this gives a counterexample to the usual Adjamagbo, or separable, formulation of the Jacobian conjecture in characteristic $2$. Stabilization yields analogous counterexamples in every dimension $n\geq 3$

</details>


### [186] [Generic ordinarity for abelian coverings of the projective line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21033)
*Régis Blache*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文证明了在特征p下，素数阶与p互质的射影直线阿贝尔覆盖是μ-普通的。通过Torelli态射，这些Hurwitz空间不可约分支的像位于某些Shimura簇中。利用这些簇的Newton多边形分层，本文证明了Hurwitz空间的通用Newton多边形与其像所在的最小Shimura簇的通用（即μ-普通）Newton多边形一致。为此，计算了射影直线上乘法特征和L-函数的通用Newton多边形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究特征p下射影直线阿贝尔覆盖的μ-普通性，以及Hurwitz空间像在Shimura簇中的Newton多边形分层性质，建立Hurwitz空间与Shimura簇之间Newton多边形的对应关系。

Method: 通过分析素数阶与p互质的射影直线阿贝尔覆盖的μ-普通性，利用Torelli态射将Hurwitz空间不可约分支映射到Shimura簇中，借助Shimura簇已知的Newton多边形分层理论，比较Hurwitz空间与最小Shimura簇的通用Newton多边形，并计算射影直线上乘法特征和L-函数的通用Newton多边形。

Result: 证明了特征p下射影直线阿贝尔覆盖（阶与p互质）是μ-普通的，且Hurwitz空间的通用Newton多边形与其像所在的最小Shimura簇的μ-普通Newton多边形一致。

Conclusion: 建立了Hurwitz空间与Shimura簇在Newton多边形分层上的联系，为理解特征p下阿贝尔覆盖的几何性质提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We show that abelian coverings of the projective line of order prime to $p$ are generically $μ$-ordinary in characteristic $p$. The images of the irreducible components of Hurwitz spaces of abelian coverings of the projective line by the Torelli morphism lie in some Shimura varieties. The stratification by Newton polygons of these varieties is known, and we show that the generic Newton polygon for the Hurwitz space coincides with the generic (or $μ$-ordinary) Newton polygon of the smallest Shimura variety that contains its image. In order to do this, we compute the generic Newton polygons for $L$-functions associated to multiplicative character sums over the projective line.

</details>

The relation between them intertwines Mikhalkin's quantum index and geometry of real and complex point sets of counted real curves. As a by-product, we suggest a new definition of quantum index, which can be used for refined invariant enumeration of real algebraic curves on surfaces in a non-toric setup.

*Stefano Canino,Cosimo Flavi,Francesco Galuppi,Yuze Luan*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了张量特征值重数的两个猜想，通过代数几何语言给出了更强、更精细的版本，并在许多新情况下证明了它们，特别是对所有 \(2 \times 2 \times \dots \times 2\) 张量。同时还建立了张量秩与零特征值重数之间的联系。

  <summary>Details</summary>
