Method: 使用代数几何语言重新表述和加强猜想，通过理论推导和特例验证（特别是 \(2 \times 2 \times \dots \times 2\) 张量）来证明。

Result: 提出了更精细的猜想形式，证明了多个新情况下的猜想成立，建立了张量秩与零特征值重数之间的关联。

Conclusion: 该工作推进了对张量特征值重数理解，并为相关领域提供了新的理论工具和结果。

Abstract: We work on two conjectures on tensor eigenvalue multiplicities. By using the language of algebraic geometry we give stronger, more refined versions of the conjectures and we prove them in many new cases, notably for all $2\times 2\times\dots\times 2$ tensors. We also establish a connection between the rank of a tensor and the multiplicities of the zero eigenvalue.

</details>


### [189] [The restricted Hitchin map of wobbly vector bundles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21457)
*Clemens Nollau*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了光滑射影曲线C上秩2稳定向量丛V的限制Hitchin映射h_V，该映射将无迹扭曲自同态φ映射为其行列式（二次微分）。证明了若V是general wobbly向量丛，则其至多有一个（相差标量）幂零扭曲自同态；进而推出h_V是有限映射并计算了次数。还证明若C非超椭圆，则h_V的像包含有简单零点的二次微分，即存在与V的扭曲自同态相关的光滑谱曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解稳定向量丛上限制Hitchin映射的性质，特别是wobbly向量丛的幂零扭曲自同态的唯一性，以及映射的有限性和次数计算。

Method: 利用代数几何方法，研究秩2稳定向量丛V的限制Hitchin映射h_V，分析幂零扭曲自同态的结构，并通过谱曲线理论建立与二次微分的关系。

Result: (1) general wobbly向量丛V至多有一个（相差标量）幂零扭曲自同态；(2) h_V是有限映射，并计算了其次数；(3) 若C非超椭圆，则h_V的像包含有简单零点的二次微分，即存在光滑谱曲线。

Conclusion: 对秩2稳定向量丛的限制Hitchin映射给出了完整的有限性和次数刻画，并揭示了非超椭圆曲线情形下光滑谱曲线的存在性。

Abstract: This article studies the restricted Hitchin map $h_V$ of a stable rank 2 vector bundle $V$ on a smooth projective curve $C$. This map associates to a trace-free twisted endomorphism $\varphi : V \to V \otimes K_C$ its determinant, which is a quadratic differential. We show that if $V$ is a general wobbly vector bundle, then it has a single nilpotent twisted endomorphism, up to scalars. As a consequence we show that $h_V$ is generically finite and we compute its degree. Furthermore, we show that if $C$ is not hyperelliptic, then the image of $h_V$ contains a quadratic differential with simple zeros. This is equivalent to saying that there is a smooth spectral curve associated to a twisted endomorphism of $V$.

</details>


### [190] [Generic degrees of real polynomial Keller maps with non-dense image](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21572)
*Piotr Migus*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有非稠密像的实Keller映射（常非零Jacobian行列式的实多项式映射）的通用次数。证明了该次数必为偶数且不等于2（至少为4），并通过三维空间中的显式构造表明每个≥4的偶数均可实现。对于n≥3，此类映射的通用次数集合恰好是所有≥4的偶数；在二维中（若平面Jacobian猜想成立）和二维以下则为空集。此外提及了Gallagher等人的相关前期工作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定具有非稠密像的实Keller映射的可能通用次数，填补该领域关于实情形下次数刻画的理论空白，并回应Jacobian猜想的相关问题。

Method: 基于Campbell定理证明次数为偶且≠2（故≥4）；利用三维空间中2026年7月Jacobian猜想反例的形变族构造出每个≥4的偶数次映射；结合维度归约分析n=1,2时的情形。

Result: 对于n≥3，实Keller映射（非稠密像）的通用次数恰为所有≥4的偶数；n=2时集合为空（若平面Jacobian猜想真）；n=1时亦为空。

Conclusion: 完整刻画了非稠密像实Keller映射的通用次数，表明高维（n≥3）情形下次数可任意大偶数，低维则受限；与复数域上已知结果（通用次数≥3）形成对比。

Abstract: For a real polynomial map of constant nonzero Jacobian determinant, a real Keller map, with non-dense image, we determine the possible generic degrees. Such a degree is necessarily even, and by Campbell's theorem different from two, hence at least four; we show conversely that every even integer $\geq4$ occurs, realized in dimension three by an explicit member of the deformation family of the July 2026 counterexample to the Jacobian conjecture. Hence for every $n\geq3$ the generic degrees of real Keller maps $\mathbb R^{n}\to\mathbb R^{n}$ with non-dense image are exactly the even integers $\geq4$; in dimension two the set is empty if the planar Jacobian conjecture holds, and in dimension one it is empty. Density is meant throughout in the Euclidean topology. An explicit degree-four real Keller map with empty real fibres along a slice of the target is due to Gallagher, and families realizing every generic degree $\geq3$ over $\mathbb C$ to Gallagher and to the base manuscript; both precede this note.

</details>

### [191] [A Single-Trace Surface Integral Equation Solver for Simulation of Open Bianisotropic Metasurfaces Described by Generalized Sheet Transition Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20659)
*Sebastian Celis Sierra,Junze Shao,Ran Zhao,Rui Chen,Partha Mondal,Hakan Bagci*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于单迹面（single-trace）表面积分方程（SIE）的求解器，结合广义片层过渡条件（GSTCs）用于模拟三维开放双各向异性超表面。该求解器仅使用单组等效表面电流，相比传统的多迹面（multi-trace）方法减少了未知量，同时保持更高精度，适用于平面和弯曲几何结构，并通过偏振旋转、完美反射和宽带吸收体等案例验证了其有效性和优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多迹面（multi-trace）公式用于模拟开放双各向异性超表面时，需要两组等效表面电流，导致未知量多、计算效率低，且需要对超表面进行人为封闭处理。因此，需要一个更高效、更简洁且不需要人工封闭的求解方法。

Method: 将超表面建模为无限薄的开放片层，利用GSTCs通过四个表面磁化率张量施加电磁场不连续性；仅用单组等效表面电流替代传统两组电流，通过SIE算子表示片层两侧的散射场并代入GSTCs；使用Rao-Wilton-Glisson（RWG）基函数对所得系统进行离散化求解；直接建模开放超表面，无需人工封闭结构。

Result: 通过与偏振旋转和完美反射的解析解对比验证了方法正确性；成功模拟了从全波仿真数据中提取磁化率张量的宽带吸收体；直接比较表明，单迹面公式相比多迹面公式误差更低，且使用的未知量显著减少。

Conclusion: 提出的单迹面SIE-GSTC求解器在模拟三维开放双各向异性超表面方面，比传统多迹面方法更高效、更精确，为超表面电磁建模提供了一种新的有力工具。

Abstract: A single-trace surface integral equation (SIE) solver incorporating generalized sheet transition conditions (GSTCs) is presented for the simulation of three-dimensional (3D) open bianisotropic metasurfaces. The metasurface is modeled as an infinitesimally thin, non-enclosing sheet across which the GSTCs enforce the electromagnetic field discontinuities through four surface susceptibility tensors. The proposed solver uses a single set of equivalent surface currents on the sheet, in place of the two sets used by prior multi-trace formulations. The scattered fields on both faces of the sheet, expressed through SIE operators acting on these currents, are substituted into the GSTCs. The resulting system of equations is then discretized using Rao--Wilton--Glisson basis functions. This solver models an open metasurface directly, without an artificial closure, and applies to both planar and curved geometries. It is validated against analytical solutions for polarization rotation and perfect reflection, and is used to model a realistic broadband absorber whose susceptibility tensors are retrieved from full-wave simulation data. A direct comparison shows that the single-trace formulation attains lower error than a multi-trace formulation while using significantly fewer unknowns.

</details>


### [192] [Matrix-free phase-field modeling of fracture in micromechanical testing simulations of inelastic materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21150)
*Fabio Di Gioacchino,Rezgar Shakeri,Zachary Atkins,Karen Stengel,Layla Ghaffari,Jeremy Thompson,Jed Brown*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文在开源固体力学库中实现了Peric & Dettmer粘弹塑性本构框架，采用支持GPU上的高阶有限元矩阵自由算子与p-多重网格预条件方法。通过引入串联组装的流变断裂单元，使得非弹性和断裂特性仅在均匀化长度尺度上相互影响。在El Capitan高性能计算原型上对合成颗粒-基体微观结构进行了拉伸和压缩数值模拟，结果再现了特征非弹性响应和裂纹扩展模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相场断裂模拟中，陡峭损伤梯度跨越弥散裂纹的求解偏好使用高阶有限元，而矩阵自由方法能提供优越性能和可扩展性。作者旨在将粘弹塑性本构框架高效实现于支持GPU加速的高阶有限元求解器中。

Method: 在开源固体力学库中实现Peric & Dettmer粘弹塑性本构框架，采用矩阵自由高阶有限元算子与p-多重网格预条件方法，引入串联组装的流变断裂单元（rheological fracture element），使非弹性和断裂特性仅在均匀化长度尺度上耦合。

Result: 在El Capitan高性能计算原型上对合成颗粒-基体微观结构进行拉伸和压缩数值模拟，成功再现了特征非弹性响应和裂纹扩展模式。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够有效模拟粘弹塑性材料中的断裂行为，且矩阵自由高阶有限元结合GPU加速具备良好的性能与可扩展性。

Abstract: Resolving steep damage gradients across diffuse cracks in the phase-field modeling of fracture favors the use of high-order finite elements, for which matrix-free methods can provide superior performance and scalability. Here, we implement the Peric & Dettmer constitutive framework for visco-elastoplastic materials in an open source solid mechanics library supporting matrix-free operators for high-order finite elements with p-multigrid preconditioning on GPUs. We introduce a rheological fracture element assembled in series so that inelastic and fracture properties can appear to affect each other only at homogenization length scales. Numerical simulations of tensile and compressive tests are conducted for synthetic particle-matrix microstructures on an El Capitan high performance computing prototype. Results are shown to reproduce characteristic inelastic responses and crack propagation patterns.

</details>


### [193] [Cycle-Consistent and Uncertainty-Aware Neural Surrogates for Tokamak Edge Plasmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21407)
*Abdourahmane Diaw,Sebastian De Pascuale,Jae-Sun Park,Ivan Paradela Perez,Jeremy D. Lore,Stefan Dasbach*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种循环一致性神经代理模型，用于托卡马克边缘等离子体的快速预测。该模型结合了条件U-Net前向模型（将5个控制参数映射到2D等离子体状态场）和基于冻结前向网络的优化反向方法。前向模型归一化RMSE低于2.6%，Pearson相关系数高于0.95；循环一致性正则化将平均循环R²从0.59提升至0.99，五个控制参数恢复的Pearson r≥0.97。模型含约4×10⁶参数，毫秒级生成2D预测，比SOLPS-ITER快5-6个数量级，支持实时控制、参数扫描、不确定性分析和数字孪生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界和偏滤器等离子体对托卡马克排热排粒子至关重要，但传统边缘模拟（如SOLPS-ITER）速度太慢，无法用于参数扫描、优化或实时控制。现有的机器学习代理大多是前向模型，无法从观测中恢复输入参数或评估预测可靠性。

Method: 提出循环一致性神经代理模型，包含：(1) 条件U-Net前向模型，将5个控制参数映射到SOLPS-ITER网格上的2D等离子体状态场；(2) 基于冻结前向网络的优化反向方法，通过循环一致性实现自监督质量检查；(3) 多层感知机集成预测电子温度和密度剖面，并提供不确定性估计。使用k-d树暖启动加速反向求解。

Result: 前向模型归一化RMSE低于2.6%，Pearson相关系数高于0.95；循环一致性正则化将平均循环R²从0.59提升至0.99且不降低前向精度；五个控制参数恢复的Pearson r≥0.97；k-d树暖启动使数据库完成率超95%（冷启动失败率约30%）；模型毫秒级生成预测，比SOLPS-ITER快5-6个数量级。

Conclusion: 该循环一致性神经代理模型在保持高精度的同时实现了极快预测速度，能够从观测中恢复输入参数并评估预测可靠性，为托卡马克边缘等离子体的实时控制、参数扫描、不确定性分析和数字孪生提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The boundary and divertor plasma govern how a tokamak exhausts power and particles, setting heat fluxes, target conditions, and the onset of detachment. Predicting these quantities is essential for operating current and future devices, but edge simulations that resolve them are too slow for parameter scans, optimization, or real-time control. Machine-learning surrogates offer a fast alternative, yet most are forward-only: they cannot recover input parameters from observations or assess the reliability of their predictions. We introduce a cycle-consistent neural surrogate for edge plasmas, combining a conditional U-Net forward model with an optimization-based inverse method built on the frozen forward network. The forward model maps five control parameters to two-dimensional plasma-state fields on the SOLPS-ITER mesh; the inverse method enforces consistency between forward and inverse predictions, a self-supervised quality check needing no ground-truth labels at inference. An ensemble of multilayer perceptrons also predicts electron temperature and density profiles at the outboard midplane and divertor targets, with uncertainty estimates that flag where more simulations are needed. The forward model achieves normalized root-mean-square errors below 2.6% and Pearson correlations above 0.95 for all fields. Cycle-consistency regularization raises the average cyclical $R^2$ from 0.59 to 0.99 without degrading forward accuracy and enables recovery of the core fueling rate; all five control parameters are recovered with Pearson $r\ge0.97$. A $k$-d tree warm start yields a database completion rate above 95%, versus roughly 30% outright failures when cold-started. With about $4\times10^6$ parameters, the model produces full 2D predictions in milliseconds, five to six orders of magnitude faster than SOLPS-ITER, enabling real-time control, parameter scans, uncertainty analysis, and digital twins.

</details>
